# <a name="essential-services-for-office"></a><span data-ttu-id="f8492-103">Osnovne storitve za Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-103">Essential services for Office</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-104">Informacije v tem članku veljajo za različico 1904 ali novejšo različico sledeče Officeove odjemalske programske opreme, ki je nameščena v računalniku s sistemom Windows:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-104">The information in this article applies to Version 1904 or later of the following Office client software installed on a computer running Windows:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-105">Office 365 ProPlus in Office 365 Business</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-105">Office 365 ProPlus and Office 365 Business</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-106">Office 365 Personal, Office 365 Home ali druge različice Officea, ki so del naročnine na Office 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-106">Office 365 Personal, Office 365 Home, or other versions of Office that are part of an Office 365 subscription.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-107">Project in Visio, ki sta vključena v nekatere naročniške pakete, kot sta paketa Project Online Professional ali Visio Online 2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-107">Project and Visio that come with some subscription plans, such as the Project Online Professional plan or Visio Online Plan 2.</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="f8492-108">Office sestavljajo aplikacije odjemalske programske opreme in povezane izkušnje, zasnovne tako, da vam omogočajo bolj učinkovito ustvarjanje, komuniciranje in sodelovanje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-108">Office consists of client software applications and connected experiences designed to enable you to create, communicate, and collaborate more effectively.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-109">Upravljate lahko številne povezane izkušnje, ki so na voljo za vas ali vaše uporabnike, če ste skrbnik v organizaciji, obstaja pa tudi nabor osnovnih storitev, ko določajo način delovanja Officea in jih tako ni mogoče onemogočiti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-109">While you can control many of the connected experiences that are available to you, or to your users if you’re the admin in your organization, there are a set of services that are essential to how Office functions and therefore cannot be disabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-110">Na primer storitev licenciranja, s katero potrdite, da imate ustrezno licenco za uporabo Officea.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-110">For example, the licensing service that confirms that you are properly licensed to use Office.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-111">Zahtevani podatki o teh storitvah so zbrani in poslani Microsoftu, ne glede na to, ali imate konfigurirane druge nastavitve pravilnika, povezane z varnostjo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-111">Required service data about these services is collected and sent to Microsoft, regardless of any other privacy-related policy settings that you have configured.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-112">Te podatke si lahko ogledate s pregledovalnikom diagnostičnih podatkov.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-112">You can see this data by using the Diagnostic Data Viewer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-113">Če želite več informacij, preberite članke:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-113">For more information, see the following:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="f8492-114">Zahtevani podatki storitev za Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-114">Required service data for Office</span></span>](required-service-data.md)
- [<span data-ttu-id="f8492-115">Uporaba pregledovalnika diagnostičnih podatkov z Officeom</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-115">Using the Diagnostic Data Viewer with Office</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/cf761ce9-d805-4c60-a339-4e07f3182855)
- [<span data-ttu-id="f8492-116">Povezane izkušnje v Officeu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-116">Connected experiences in Office</span></span>](connected-experiences.md)

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-117">Če ste skrbnik v svoji organizaciji, vas bo morda zanimalo to:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-117">If you’re the admin for your organization, you might also be interested in the following:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="f8492-118">Pregled kontrolnikov zasebnosti za Office 365 ProPlus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-118">Overview of privacy controls for Office 365 ProPlus</span></span>](overview-privacy-controls.md)
- [<span data-ttu-id="f8492-119">Uporaba nastavitev pravilnika za upravljanje kontrolnikov zasebnosti za Office365 ProPlus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-119">Use policy settings to manage privacy controls for Office 365 ProPlus</span></span>](manage-privacy-controls.md)

## <a name="list-of-essential-services-for-office"></a><span data-ttu-id="f8492-120">Seznam osnovnih storitev za Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-120">List of essential services for Office</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-121">V tej tabeli si lahko ogledate seznam osnovnih storitev za Office in opis posameznih storitev.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-121">The following table provides a list of the essential services for Office and a description of each service.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="f8492-122">**Storitev**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-122">**Service**</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="f8492-123">**Opis**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-123">**Description**</span></span>  |
| ------ | ---- |
| [<span data-ttu-id="f8492-124">Preverjanje pristnosti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-124">Authentication</span></span>](#authentication-events) | <span data-ttu-id="f8492-125">Preverjanje pristnosti je storitev, ki je na voljo v različnih platformah, s katero lahko preverite veljavnost identitete uporabnika v Officeu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-125">Authentication is a cross-platform service that validates your Office user identity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-126"> S to storitvijo lahko omogočite vpis v Office, aktivirate licenco za Office, dostopate do datotek, shranjenih v oblaku in zagotovite stalne izkušnje v sejah ter napravah, v katerih je nameščen Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-126"> It is required to enable you to sign in to Office, activate your Office license, access your files stored in the cloud, and provides a consistent experience across Office sessions and your devices.</span></span>    |
| [<span data-ttu-id="f8492-127">Zagon s klikom</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-127">Click-to-Run</span></span>](#click-to-run-events) | <span data-ttu-id="f8492-128">Zagon s klikom je tehnologija namestitev, ki se uporablja za namestitev in posodobitev Officea v sistemu Windows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-128">Click-to-Run is the installation technology used to install and update Office on Windows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-129">Preveri, ali so na voljo nove različice Officea, in če je na voljo nova različica, jo prenese ter namesti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-129">It checks for new versions of Office, and when a new version is available, downloads and installs it.</span></span><span data-ttu-id="f8492-130"> Zagon s klikom zazna potrebo, prenese in namesti posodobitve za Office, med drugim tudi varnostne posodobitve.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-130"> Click-to-Run will detect the need for, perform the download of, and install Office updates, including security updates.</span></span>     |
| [<span data-ttu-id="f8492-131">Izboljšana konfiguracijska storitev (ECS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-131">Enhanced Configuration Service (ECS)</span></span>](#experimentation-and-configuration-service-ecs-events) | <span data-ttu-id="f8492-132">Storitev ECS Microsoftu omogoča vnovično konfiguracijo namestitev Office, brez potrebe po vnovični uvedbi Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-132">ECS provides Microsoft the ability to reconfigure Office installations without the need for you to redeploy Office.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-133">Uporablja se za nadzor postopnega izdajanja funkcij ali posodobitev. Učinek izdajanja pa lahko nadzorujete z zbranimi diagnostičnimi podatki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-133">It is used to control the gradual rollout of features or updates, while the impact of the rollout is monitored from diagnostic data being collected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-134">Storitev se prav tako uporablja za preprečevanje varnostnih težav in težav z učinkovitostjo delovanja funkcije oziroma posodobitve.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-134">It is also used to mitigate security or performance issues with a feature or update.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-135">Storitev ECS prav tako podpira spremembe konfiguracije, povezane z diagnostičnimi podatki, ki zagotovijo zbiranje ustreznih dogodkov.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-135">In addition, ECS supports configuration changes related to diagnostic data to help ensure that the appropriate events are being collected.</span></span> |
| [<span data-ttu-id="f8492-136">Licenciranje</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-136">Licensing</span></span>](#licensing-events)     | <span data-ttu-id="f8492-137">Licenciranje je storitev v oblaku, ki podpira aktivacijo Office za nove namestitve in ohrani licenco v vaših napravah, po tem, ko ste aktivirali Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-137">Licensing is a cloud-based service that supports your Office activation for new installations and maintains the license on your devices after Office has been activated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-138">Registrira posamezne naprave in aktivira Office, preveri stanje vaše naročnine na Office in upravlja vaše ključe izdelkov.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-138">It registers each of your devices and activates Office, checks the status of your Office subscription, and manages your product keys.</span></span>    |
| [<span data-ttu-id="f8492-139">Konfiguracija storitev</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-139">Services Configuration</span></span>](#services-configuration-events)  | <span data-ttu-id="f8492-140">Konfiguracija storitev omogoča posodobitve konfiguracijskih nastavitev za Office za omogočanje oziroma onemogočanje odjemalskih funkcij.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-140">Services Configuration provides the ability to make updates to Office configuration settings to enable or disable client features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-141">Storitev se aktivira vsakič, ko se zažene Officeova aplikacija, in zagotavlja podrobnosti o drugih konfiguracijah ter storitvah v Officeu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-141">It is called every time an Office application is started and provides details about other Office configurations and services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-142">Storitve konfiguracije prav tako nadzorujejo, katere storitve so opredeljene kot osnovne storitve.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-142">Services Configuration also controls which services are designated as essential services.</span></span>  |
| [<span data-ttu-id="f8492-143">Telemetrija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-143">Telemetry </span></span>](#telemetry-events)  | <span data-ttu-id="f8492-144">Storitev telemetrije se uporablja za zbiranje diagnostičnih podatkov iz Officeovih aplikacij.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-144">The Telemetry service is used to collect diagnostic data from Office applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-145">Omogoča zbiranje diagnostičnih podatkov, ki jih ustvarja Office (zahtevanih in izbirnih diagnostičnih podatkov).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-145">It enables the collection of the diagnostic data generated by Office, both required and optional diagnostic data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-146">Storitev je prav tako odgovorna za zbiranje dela diagnostičnih podatkov storitve za zahtevano storitev za Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-146">It is also responsible for the collection of the service diagnostic data portion of required service data for Office.</span></span>  |

## <a name="events-and-data-fields-for-essential-services-for-office"></a><span data-ttu-id="f8492-147">Dogodki in podatkovna polja za osnovne storitve za Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-147">Events and data fields for essential services for Office</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-148">V naslednjih razdelkih boste naleteli na:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-148">The next sections provide the following information:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="f8492-149">Seznam dogodkov za posamezne osnovne storitve</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-149">A list of events for each essential service</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f8492-150">Opis posameznih dogodkov</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-150">A description of each event</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f8492-151">Seznam podatkovnih polj v posameznih dogodkih</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-151">A list of data fields in each event</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="f8492-152">Opis posameznih podatkovnih polj</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-152">A description of each data field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-153">Te dogodke si lahko ogledate s pregledovalnikom diagnostičnih podatkov.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-153">You can see these events by using the Diagnostic Data Viewer.</span></span>



## <a name="authentication-events"></a><span data-ttu-id="f8492-154">Dogodki preverjanja pristnosti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-154">Authentication events</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-155">Ti dogodki diagnostičnih podatkov se zberejo, ko Office poskuša pridobiti žeton za preverjanje pristnosti (na tih način ali prek poziva).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-155">These diagnostic data events are collected when Office attempts to acquire an authentication token, either silently or through prompting.</span></span>

### <a name="officeidentityfbapromptwin32"></a><span data-ttu-id="f8492-156">Office.Identity.FbaPromptWin32</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-156">Office.Identity.FbaPromptWin32</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-157">Dogodki se zberejo, ko Office uporabniku prikaže poziv za vpis s preverjanjem pristnosti z obrazci.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-157">Collected when Office shows the user a Forms-Based-Auth sign-in prompt.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-158">Poleg tihih pridobitev žetonom se s pozivi za preverjanje pristnosti ugotovi, ali je za uporabnika aktivirano stanje prekinjenega preverjanja pristnosti. Uporabnik se tako nahaja v stanju odjemalca brez povezave, v najslabšem primeru pa prekinjeno preverjanje pristnosti lahko povzroči pridobivanje licence in onemogoči odjemalca v celoti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-158">Along with silent token acquisitions, authentication prompts is used to determine if user is in a broken authentication state which, for the user, results in what is essentially an Offline Client state, or in the worst case, broken authentication may prevent license acquisition and result in a completely unusable client.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-159">Pozivi za vpis s preverjanjem pristnosti z obrazci se uporabljajo za nekatere scenarije preverjanja pristnosti na mestu uporabe, vendar tega običajno ne želimo, ker bi uporabniki morali uporabljati sodobno preverjanje pristnosti zaradi varnostnih ranljivosti, povezanih s preverjanjem pristnosti z obrazci.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-159">Forms-Based-Auth (FBA) sign-in prompts are used for some on-premises authentication scenarios and typically we want to make sure this isn’t happening, as everyone should be using Modern-Auth because of security vulnerabilities associated with FBA.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-160">**Zbrana so sledeča polja:**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-160">**The following fields are collected:**</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-161">**AuthScheme** – uporabljena shema za preverjanje pristnosti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-161">**AuthScheme** - the authentication scheme used</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-162">**DocumentUrlHash** – zahteva za šifrirani URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-162">**DocumentUrlHash** - an encrypted URL requesting</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-163">**EndTag** – oznaka, pri kateri se zaključi obrazec za preverjanje pristnosti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-163">**EndTag** - the tag where FBA form is completed</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-164">**Flags** – zastarelo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-164">**Flags** - Obsolete</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-165">**FlowTag** – oznaka, pri kateri se začne obrazec za preverjanje pristnosti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-165">**FlowTag** - the tag where FBA form is started</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-166">**LastError** – vrnjena koda napake</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-166">**LastError** – the error code returned</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-167">**PromptEndTime** – čas, ko se je poziv končal</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-167">**PromptEndTime** - the time when then prompt ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-168">**PromptStartTime** – čas, ko se je poziv začel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-168">**PromptStartTime** - the time when the prompt started</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-169">**Result** – ali je bilo preverjanje pristnosti uspešno</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-169">**Result** - whether the authentication succeeded</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-170">**SessionEndTime** – čas, ko se konča seja dogodka</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-170">**SessionEndTime** – the time when the event session ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-171">**Timeout** – čas, ko je potekla časovna omejitev poziva</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-171">**Timeout** - the time when the prompt timed out</span></span>

### <a name="officeidentitysignoutevent"></a><span data-ttu-id="f8492-172">Office.Identity.SignOutEvent</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-172">Office.Identity.SignOutEvent</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-173">Dogodki se zberejo, ko se uporabnik izpiše iz Officea.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-173">Collected when a user signs out of Office.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-174">Če veste, da se je uporabnik izpisal, lahko pričakovano razvrstite druge dogodke, na primer pozive, da bodo ti dogodki lahko pravilno izračunani v metriki zanesljivosti/pripravljenosti na odpremo. Prav tako se lahko izognete opozorilom oziroma razveljavljanju gradenj ob lažni predpostavki, da je uporabnik deležen nepričakovanih pozivov za vpis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-174">Knowing the user is signed-out makes it possible to classify other events, such as prompts, as expected, so those events can be correctly computed in reliability / ship-readiness metrics and avoid alerting or rolling back builds on the faulty premise that the user is experiencing unexpected sign-in prompts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-175">Zbrana so sledeča polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-175">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-176">**FlowEndTime** – čas, ko se konča izpis</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-176">**FlowEndTime** - the time when the sign out action ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-177">**FlowStartTime** – čas, ko se začne izpis</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-177">**FlowStartTime** - the time when the sign out action started</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-178">**IdentityErrorState** – stanje napake identitete pri izpisu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-178">**IdentityErrorState** - any identity error state during sign out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-179">**IdentityHashedUniqueId** – šifrirani ID identitete pri izpisu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-179">**IdentityHashedUniqueId** - the encrypted identity ID being signed out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-180">**IdentityProviderType** – ponudnik identitete za identiteto, za katero poteka izpis</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-180">**IdentityProviderType** - the identity provider of the identity being signed out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-181">**IdentityUniqueID** – ID identitete, za katero poteka izpis</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-181">**IdentityUniqueID** - the identity ID being signed out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-182">**SessionEndTime** – čas, ko se konča seja dogodka</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-182">**SessionEndTime** - the time when the event session ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-183">**SignOutUserAction** – ponazarja, da je uporabnik začel postopek izpisa</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-183">**SignOutUserAction** - Indicates the user initiates the sign out action</span></span>

### <a name="officeidentitysspipromptwin32"></a><span data-ttu-id="f8492-184">Office.Identity.SspiPromptWin32</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-184">Office.Identity.SspiPromptWin32</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-185">Dogodki se zberejo, ko Office uporabniku prikaže poziv za vpis prek vmesnika SSPI v sistemu Windows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-185">Collected when Office shows the user a Windows SSPI sign-in prompt.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-186">Poleg tihih pridobitev žetonov se s pozivi za preverjanje pristnosti ugotovi, ali je za uporabnika aktivirano stanje prekinjenega preverjanja pristnosti. Rezultat tega je stanje odjemalca brez povezave.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-186">Along with silent token acquisitions, authentication prompts determine whether a user is in a broken authentication state, which results in an Offline Client state.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-187">Prekinjeno preverjanje pristnosti lahko prepreči pridobitev licence in onemogoči odjemalca v celoti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-187">Broken authentication may prevent license acquisition and result in a completely unusable client.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-188">Pozivi vmesnika SSPI v sistemu Windows se uporabljajo za preverjanje pristnosti z Exchangeom (za sinhronizacijo pošte), ko vir za Exchange uporabnika ni bil nastavljen za večkratno preverjanje pristnosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-188">Windows SSPI prompts are used for authenticating with Exchange (for mail synchronizing) when the user's Exchange resource hasn't been setup for multi-factor authentication.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-189">Ti dogodki se skupaj z dogodki imenskega prostora Office.MATS uporabljajo za te namene:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-189">These events, along with the Office.MATS namespace events, are used for the following purposes:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-190">1\) Ugotovite, ali odjemalci lahko uspešno pridobijo žeton za preverjanje pristnosti oziroma je za njih aktivirano stanje prekinjenega preverjanja pristnosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-190">1\) Identify whether clients can successfully obtain an authentication token or have entered a broken authentication state.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-191">2\) Ovrednotite, ali je prišlo do sprememb v odjemalcu, oziroma je v storitvah prišlo do kritičnih regresij glede izkušnje in zanesljivosti pri preverjanju pristnosti uporabnika.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-191">2\) Evaluate whether changes that have occurred on the client or services have resulted in critical regressions in the user's authentication experience and reliability</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-192">3\) Ko se pojavijo napake, ti signali iz odgovorne komponente (koda odjemalca za Office, knjižnice za preverjanje pristnosti ali storitve avtoritete) oddajo pomembne kode napak, ki se jih lahko uporabi za triažo, diagnosticiranje ali odpravljanje napak.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-192">3\) When failures occur, these signals emit important failure codes from the responsible component (Office client code, authentication libraries, or authority services) which can be used for triage, diagnosis and mitigation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-193">4\) Ti signali ponazarjajo različne pripravljenosti na odpremo in nadzirajo stanja, zaradi katerih se aktivirajo opozorila. Na ta način naši inženirji lahko hitro ukrepajo in skrajšajo čas za odpravljanje kritičnih težav blokiranja uporabnikov.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-193">4\) These signals power various ship readiness and health monitors which fire alerts so our engineers can engage quickly and reduce the time to mitigation of critical user-blocking failures</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-194">Zbrana so sledeča polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-194">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-196">**AuthScheme** – uporabljena shema za preverjanje pristnosti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-196">**AuthScheme** - the authentication scheme used</span></span>

### <a name="officematsactionofficewin32-officematsactionofficewinrt"></a><span data-ttu-id="f8492-244">Office.MATS.actionofficewin32, Office.MATS.actionofficewinrt</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-244">Office.MATS.actionofficewin32, Office.MATS.actionofficewinrt</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-246">Microsoftov telemetrični sistem za preverjanje pristnosti (MATS) se zbere, ko Office poskuša pridobiti žeton za preverjanje pristnosti (na tih način ali prek poziva).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-246">Microsoft Auth Telemetry System (MATS) is collected when Office attempts to acquire an authentication token, either silently or through prompting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-247">Če pridobitev ni uspešna, so vključeni tudi podatki o napakah.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-247">When acquisition attempts fail, error information is included.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-248">S temi dogodki se naši uporabniki lahko izognejo stanju prekinjenega preverjanja pristnosti tako, da:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-248">These events help our users avoid entering broken authentication states by:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-249">1\) Ugotovijo, ali odjemalci lahko uspešno pridobijo žeton za preverjanje pristnosti oziroma je za njih aktivirano stanje prekinjenega preverjanja pristnosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-249">1\) Identifying whether clients can successfully obtain an authentication token or have entered a broken authentication state.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-250">2\) Ovrednotijo, kdaj je prišlo do sprememb v odjemalcu ali storitvah, ali je prišlo do kritičnih regresij glede izkušnje in zanesljivosti pri preverjanju pristnosti uporabnika.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-250">2\) Evaluate when changes occur on the client or services, whether they result in critical regressions in the user's authentication experience and reliability</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-251">3\) Ko se pojavijo napake, ti signali iz odgovorne komponente (koda odjemalca za Office, knjižnice za preverjanje pristnosti ali storitve avtoritete) oddajo pomembne kode napak, ki se jih lahko uporabi za triažo, diagnosticiranje ali odpravljanje napak.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-251">3\) When failures occur, these signals emit important failure codes from the responsible component (Office client code, authentication libraries, or authority services) which can be used for triage, diagnosis and mitigation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-252">4\) Ti signali ponazarjajo različne pripravljenosti na odpremo in nadzirajo stanja, zaradi katerih se aktivirajo opozorila. Na ta način naši inženirji lahko hitro ukrepajo in skrajšajo čas za odpravljanje kritičnih težav.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-252">4\) These signals power various ship readiness and health monitors which fire alerts so our engineers can engage quickly and reduce the time to mitigation of critical failures.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-253">Zbrana so sledeča polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-253">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-254">**Actiontype** – katera vrsta knjižnice za preverjanje pristnosti se uporabi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-254">**Actiontype** - Which authentication library is used</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-255">**Appaudience** – ali je aplikacija namenjena za notranjo oziroma zunanjo uporabo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-255">**Appaudience** - Is the app build for internal or external use</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-256">**Appforcedprompt** – ali aplikacija preglasi predpomnilnik in vsili prikaz poziva</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-256">**Appforcedprompt** - Did the app override cache and force a prompt to be shown</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-259">**Askedforcreds** – ali ja aplikacija uporabnika pozvala za vnos poverilnic za to dejanje</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-259">**Askedforcreds** - Did the application ask the user to enter credentials for this action</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-260">**Authoutcome** – ali je bil poskus preverjanja pristnosti uspešen, ni bil uspešen oziroma je bil preklican</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-260">**Authoutcome** - Did the authentication attempt succeed, fail, or was cancelled</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-338">**Scenarioid** – GUID.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-338">**Scenarioid** – GUID.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f8492-339">Enemu scenariju lahko pripada več dogodkov.   - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-341">**Sessionid** – GUID za prepoznavanje seje zagona</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-341">**Sessionid** - GUID identifying the boot session</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-342">**Skdver** – različica odjemalskega kompleta za razvoj programske opreme MATS, uporabljena za ustvarjanje teh podatkov</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-342">**Skdver** - Version of MATS client SDK used to produce this data</span></span>

### <a name="officetelemetryvolumetrackingdata"></a><span data-ttu-id="f8492-2363">Office.Telemetry.VolumeTrackingData</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-2363">Office.Telemetry.VolumeTrackingData</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-2364">Metrika za sledenje količine dogodkov za dogodke telemetrije</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-2364">Event volume tracking metrics for telemetry events</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-2365">Zbrana so sledeča polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-2365">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-2366">**EventThreshold** – največje število primerkov za posamezen dogodek, ki ga lahko pošljete v časovnem oknu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-2366">**EventThreshold** - The maximum number of instances of a single event that can be sent in a window of time.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-2367">**HighestEventCount** – najvišje število primerkov za posamezen dogodek, poslan v tem oknu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-2367">**HighestEventCount** - The highest number of instances of a single event sent this window.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-2368">**HighestEventName** – ime dogodka z najvišjim številom primerkov v tem oknu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-2368">**HighestEventName** - The name of the event with the highest number of instances in this window.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-2369">**TimeWindowInSeconds** – trajanje okna v sekundah</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-2369">**TimeWindowInSeconds** - The duration of the window in seconds.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-2370">**TotalEvents** – skupno število dogodkov, poslanih v oknu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-2370">**TotalEvents** - The total number of events sent during the window.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-2371">**UniqueEvents** – število enoličnih dogodkov, poslanih v oknu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-2371">**UniqueEvents** - The number of unique events sent during a window.</span></span>

### <a name="officetelemetrywritepayloadstodisk"></a><span data-ttu-id="f8492-2372">Office.Telemetry.WritePayloadsToDisk</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-2372">Office.Telemetry.WritePayloadsToDisk</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-2373">Preveri, ali določeni podedovani deli cevovoda delujejo v platformah, ki jih še vedno uporabljajo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-2373">Verifies certain parts of legacy pipeline are working on platforms that still use it.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f8492-2374">Zbrana so sledeča polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-2374">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="f8492-2375">**DetachedDuration** – ločeno trajanje v mikrosekundah</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f8492-2375">**DetachedDuration** - Detached duration in microseconds</span></span>
